# 文档：Gravitas

- 类别：duplicants
- 标识：gravitas
- 来源：wiki/Gravitas

Gravitas was an Earth technology company that conducted experimental and often controversial projects with great success. However, it was destroyed along with the rest of the Earth during the events instigated at Gravitas Facility and leading up to the game.

Company
The logo of Gravitas was a stylized strand of DNA, shaped to look like an hourglass. The Gravitas Facility lobby reception desk has this logo prominently displayed. Products Gravitas sold include the Thermo Nullifier, the Printing Pod, and the matter manipulator tools, that duplicants use to do errands. Most of the critters and plants are also bio-engineered by Gravitas.

Personnel
Those are the employees of Gravitas as they mentioned in the Lore of the game. Some of them also appear in the game as derived duplicants.

Director Jacquelyn Stern
Position: Director
Aliases: Jackie, Director
Security code: A001
Appears in: Moved Rats, Employee Processing, Revisited Numbers, Nucleoid Article, Byproduct Notes, Possible Applications, Planetary Echoes, Director's Notes, Re: Implant Database_Request, Re: Objectionable Request, Campus Newspaper Article, Time's Arrow Thoughts
Mentioned in: Personal Journal: B556, Pipedream, Personal Journal: B556, Duplicant Memory Solution, Polite Request, Preliminary Calculations, Personal Journal: B111

The director of Gravitas Facility. Although she was a typical college student when she was going to school with Olivia, as time passes she is increasingly consumed with the Time's Bow, perhaps pressed by the need to solve humankind's problems, and takes severe risks rather than allow Dr. Broussard to take more time to do research. It is possible that the Director was directly related to the fracturing of Earth, starting the events of the game.

Jacquelyn Stern's office smelled strongly of artificial lemon, and the newspaper clipping of her and Olivia's time travellers' party was hung on the wall. She kept a picture of herself and Olivia at their college graduation in her desk, and wore thick glasses. She had a secret taste for gingersnaps.

Dr. Olivia Broussard
Position: Head of Bioengineering Department
Aliases: brainmap.AI
Security code: B111
Appears in: Employee Processing, Moved Rats, Pipedream, Revisited Numbers, Sunflower Seeds, Planetary Echoes, Campus Newspaper Article, Re: Objectionable Request, Re: Have you seen this?, Re: Implant Database Request, Log entries, Research Notes, Personal Journal: B111
Mentioned in: Personal Journal: A046, Personal Journal: B556, Welcome, New Employee

Dr. Olivia Broussard was the head of the Gravitas Bioengineering Department, and college friend of Director Stern. When she was onboarded, a copy of her genetic makeup was taken. At first she was deferential to the Director's orders, but later on she was increasingly uncomfortable with the ethical situation, and eventually quit from the colony project. She displayed a fond spot for some duplicant lab rats she had printed. Later on, the Colony AI is revealed to have been based on Dr. Broussard's brainmap.

Olivia and Jacquelyn threw a time travellers' party when they were undergrads, though nobody showed up. Olivia didn't seem bothered by this turn of events, stating that "It just meant more snacks for us!".

Dr. Holland
Position: Technician, possibly Engineering
Security code: B556
Appears in: Ants, Personal Journal: B556
Mentioned in: Re: dr. holland's dog, Personal Journal: B111

Dr. Holland was an employee at Gravitas, likely in the Engineering department. He worked on battery capacity and power, and was severely stressed by the need to prove results, to the point of having some minor mental breakdowns. The Director's personal attention didn't help matters, either. However, Dr. Broussard pushed him to take a break, and he felt much better afterwards. Also, he got a pet dog.

Dr. Banhi Ansari
Position: Robotics Department
Aliases: Pipsqueak, Banhi
Mentioned in: Personal Journal: B835

May have been the "B.A." mentioned by the Robot Arm Artifact.

Dr. Devon Ross
Aliases: Devon
Mentioned in: Re: devon's bloggg, Vacation Request Approved

Dr. Ross was an employee at Gravitas. They ran a food blog, Toast of the Town, that was nominated for the Blogjam Awards. Dr. Summers followed that blog.

The dupe Devon is referred to as "they" and their gender marker is X, and Dr. Mason is referred to as "they" in Re: devon's bloggg, so it's likely that Dr. Mason was nonbinary. In addition, dupes are referred to in a de-individualizing manner, such as "a Catalina", "this Burt", "Frankies are", "every Ren", they are often referred to as one of mutliple, but Devon's description is in singular form and still uses "they" to refer to them.

Dr. Ellie Jones
Position: Information and Statistics Department
Aliases: Ellie
Security code: A435
Appears in: Office Cake, Revisited Numbers, Results from Atomicon, Re: devon's bloggg, Hiiiii!, Re: dr. holland.27s dog, Re: MY PENS, Preliminary Calculations, Re: omg the janitor, The Laws of Thermodynamics

Dr. Jones was an employee at Gravitas, working in the Information and Statistics department, possibly as the department head. She was a notorious gossip, as evidenced by her email exchanges with Dr. Summers, and greatly enjoyed glittery things.

Dr. Joshua Summers
Position: Information and Statistics Department
Aliases: Joshua
Appears in: Office Cake, Re: devon's bloggg, Re:_dr. holland's dog, Re: omg the janitor

Dr. Summers was an employee at Gravitas, working in the Information and Statistics department. He was a friend of Dr. Jones, and often talked with her over email. Dr. Summers enjoyed Dr. Holland's food blog.

Dr. M. Sklodowska
Position: Physics Department
Aliases: Marie or Mi-Ma? (More likely Marie, as Sklodowska is the maiden name of Marie Curie)
Security code: A046
Appears in: Personal Journal: A046, RE: To Otto - Spec Changes,

Dr. Sklodowska was an employee at Gravitas, working in the Physics Department. She was one of the older employees working there, but was hired relatively recently. She had trouble using electronic devices, including email, and her friend Mr. Kraus helped teach her how to properly reply to an email thread.

Dr. Nikola Techna
Aliases: Nikola
Mentioned in: Email_content#Hiiiii.21: Hiiiii!

Dr. Techna was an employee at Gravitas. He had spiky blonde hair and stole food from the communal fridge. Dr. Jones insinuated that she would delete his files if he didn't stop.

Mr. Otto Kraus
Position: Physics Department
Aliases: Otto
Security code: B327
Appears in: Office Cake, Personal Journal: B327, Personal Journal: B556, RE: To Otto - Spec Changes, Spec Changes
Mentioned in: Personal Journal: A046, The Laws of Thermodynamics
Possibly appears in: New Security System?, They Stole Our DNA

Mr. Otto Kraus was a PhD student and an employee at Gravitas. He was insecure and anxious, and had crippling student loan debt. He asked Dr. Summers why he was friends Dr. Jones, thinking she is mean.

Mr. Gunderson
Position: Janitor
Aliases: Stinky
Appears in: Cleaning up the Mess
Mentioned in: Re: omg the janitor

Mr. "Stinky" Gunderson was a janitor at Gravitas. His nickname alludes to the fact that he tends to always have sweaty armpits and strong body odor. He was aware of the fact that Gravitas was conducting cloning experiments. Dr. Summers considered him a good janitor.

Personnel Coordinator
Position: Personnel Coordinator
Appears in: Welcome, New Employee, Re: Have you seen this?

The Personnel Coordinator at Gravitas, whose name we do not know. They expressed concern about the company's bad PR to the Director, but she instructed her to ignore the articles and decline to comment when asked for statements.

Dr. "Bubbles" Bubare
Position: Bioengineering Department
Aliases: Bubbles
Security code: B835
Appears in: Personal Journal: B835, In Space

Dr. "Bubbles" was an employee in the Bioengineering Department. She was college friends with Dr. "Pipsqueak" Ansari, who is also the reason the staff at Gravitas took to calling her Bubbles. Though she was aghast at the nickname at first, she and Dr. Ansari quickly reconnected and became best friends. Dr. Ansari also taught Bubbles how to do her hairstyle. Incidentally, the duplicant Bubbles has the same hair style as the duplicant Banhi.

Dr. Ashkan Seyed Ali
Position: unknown (most likely in robotics, possibly in ai development or bioengineering)
Aliases: Ashkan
Security code: unknown
Appears in: A Paradox, Pristine Fossil Artifact

Dr. Ali wrote a paper in which he noted a robot behaved like "a puppy that was lost in a teleportation experiment weeks ago", which alerted Dr. Broussard, who reviewed his work. Therefore he blew the cover-up of the Teleportation experiments which Jackie kept secret from Dr. Broussard since she disagrees with their moral and ethical implications.
He is also noted as creating a technique to artificially create fossils, which is dubbed "The Ali Method"

Dr. Robin Nisbet
Position: unknown
Aliases: Nisbet
Appears in: Magma Lamp Artifact

Designs for the Magma Lamp are attributed to Dr. Nisbet.

Dr. Travaldo Farrington
Position: unknown (presumably in nuclear physics)
Aliases: Travaldo
Appears in: Radioactive Mood Ring Artifact

Dr. Farrington wrote his PhD thesis on "Novelty Uses for Radiochromatic Dyes".

Dr. Dylan "Nails" Winslow
Position: unknown
Aliases: Nails
Appears in: Rubik's Cube Artifact

Dr. Winslow was once a regional Rubik's Cube champion.

Dr. Ren Sato
Position: unknown
Aliases: Ren
Appears in: Moldavite Artifact

Dr. Sato once owned a piece of rare, museum-grade moldavite before it was stolen by an unknown individual. He suspected Director Stern but never was able to prove it.

Dr. Harold P. Moreson
Position: Geology department
Aliases: Harold
Mentioned in: Tornado Rock Artifact

Dr. Moreson theorized that the tornado rock could have been a geode that failed to form any crystals inside. the paper that he wrote about the subject is stated to be a likely factor in him being hired at Gravitas.

---

# 文档：Incapacitated

- 类别：duplicants
- 标识：incapacitated
- 来源：wiki/Incapacitated

Entities become Incapacitated when they reach 0 health.

Incapacitated duplicants must be brought to a triage cot, or they will die.

Incapacitated duplicants must be brought to a triage cot by another duplicant.

Other entities than dupes will drop meat upon killing.

---

# 文档：Skills

- 类别：duplicants
- 标识：skills
- 来源：wiki/Skills

.]]
As Duplicants work in the colony, they will gain skill points to upgrade their attributes and gain new abilities. Skill points are spent through using the Skills menu.

Mechanics
After reaching an XP threshold the duplicant will gain a skill point.
Spending a skill point is instant and semi-permanent. Duplicants will visit the Printing Pod to master the skill.
Some jobs grant new abilities to dupes, some only increase attributes.
Morale expectations are a sum of the morale costs of all the duplicant's skills. A duplicant without any skills has no morale expectations.
Duplicant interests will show a heart icon and grant 1 bonus morale when mastered. This allows tier 1 skills to be effectively free.
Skills may be reset by using the Skill Scrubber.

Skill Tree

Hats
Every mastered skill rewards a hat, which can be accessed after learning the respective skill in the skills screen. Hats are purely cosmetic and duplicants may freely switch between any hat they own.

Surf'n'Turf
Frost Burger

History

---

# 文档：Berry Sludge

- 类别：food
- 标识：berry sludge
- 来源：wiki/Berry_Sludge

Berry Sludge is a food item made from 5 Sleet Wheat Grain and 1600 kcal Bristle Berry. It has a Food Quality of Good (+3) and provides 4,000 kcal.

Berry Sludge is one of the best mid-tier foods, and is superior in quality to both Frost Bun and Gristle Berry from Electric Grill.

Its unlimited shelf life allows it to be stored outside of the regular food storage. It is the only duplicant-craftable food that cannot spoil.

There are no recipes using Berry Sludge as an ingredient to create more sophisticated food.

Tips
In the DLC, Berry Sludges are an excellent recipe for long term rocket ventures, due to being everlasting as well as having a decent morale bonus. Pickled Meal and Grubfruit Preserve are relatively easier to produce, but only last 32 cycles instead of forever (And in case of Pickled Meal, its quality is Grisly (-1), a significant drawback).

Trivia
Its inability to spoil may be a reference to the myth that fruit cake lasts forever, though it is more likely to be inspired by pemmican.

History

---

# 文档：Bristle Berry

- 类别：food
- 标识：bristle berry
- 来源：wiki/Bristle_Berry

A Bristle Berry is the fruit of the Bristle Blossom plant.

Recipes
The Microbe Musher can cook it into Berry Sludge.
The Electric Grill can cook it into Gristle Berry.
The Juicer produces a drink from it, that can augment the morale and strength attributes.

---

# 文档：Consumables

- 类别：food
- 标识：consumables
- 来源：wiki/Consumables

The Consumables Chart allows precise control over which Duplicants may consume what Food and Medicine. It can be accessed by either pressing the F key or clicking the "Consumables" button at the top of the screen.

Usage
After opening, the chart is displayed. In the leftmost column, each Duplicant's head, name, skill points and Morale are displayed in individual rows. These can be sorted by name and by morale. The first row allows setting up consumables for new Duplicants.

Right to that column is the main grid: The topmost row contains an icon of every food and medicine item the colony has discovered or manufactured already. Hovering over them displays a tooltip containing their name, available calories/units of that item, morale bonus if consumed and a short description. Consumables are grouped by morale bonus (Food) and effect (Medicine). If the amount of those items is too large to be displayed in this section, then the displayed scrollbar or the mouse wheel can be used to scroll along the list.

Below each item is a column of checkboxes, corresponding to the Duplicant in each row. Their colour is white for medicine and "Grisly" quality foods but gets more saturated with purple the higher the morale bonus of that food is. If a checkbox is ticked, the Duplicant whose row it is in, is allowed to consume the item whose column the checkbox is in. Clicking a checkbox toggles whether or not the Duplicant is allowed to consume an item. This is represented by a tick in the box. Whole columns can be toggled by clicking the respective food icon. Whole rows can also be toggled by pressing the rightmost button in each row. Those are displayed constantly in the rightmost section. Clicking the button in the top right toggles all checkboxes.

Tips
It is not advised to deselect Curative Tablet for any Duplicant, as any Duplicant can also get Food Poisoning.
If Vitamin Chews or Immuno Reducers are available, it is a good idea to only allow Duplicants working in germy environments to take these so they aren't wasted.
Raw or unprocessed food that is going to be Cooked (for example raw Meat) should generally be deselected, so Duplicants only eat the higher quality food item, if it is available. This prevents a Morale penalty and possible Stress build-up.
Duplicants will eat Basic Rad Pills whether they already are irradiated or not. It is therefore advisable to deselect and manually control access to rad pills.

---

# 文档：Cooked Seafood

- 类别：food
- 标识：cooked seafood
- 来源：wiki/Cooked_Seafood

The Cooked Seafood is a food item made from Pacu Fillet or Raw Shellfish. It provides 1,600 kcal with food quality of .

Recipes
Inside the Gas Range, Cooked Seafood can be cooked into:
Surf'n'Turf

Notes
Compared with Pacu Fillet or Raw Shellfish, Cooked Seafood provides more calories and higher food quality.
Cooked Seafood was called Cooked Fish before the Fast Friends Update, and also used to have different artwork prior to that update.

Gallery
History

# 文档：Curried Beans

- 类别：food
- 标识：curried beans
- 来源：wiki/Curried_Beans

Curried Beans are a food item made at the Gas Range with Tonic Root and Nosh Beans. It provides 5,000 kcal with food quality of  and the unique Hot Stuff effect, which grants +3 Athletics, +3 Strength, +1 Sneeziness, and +5% stress  for 2 cycles.

There are no recipes using Curried Beans as an ingredient to create even more sophisticated food.

For long-time storage it can be kept in  environment while being  or be dehydrated.

History

---

# 文档：Dried Berry Pie

- 类别：food
- 标识：dried berry pie
- 来源：wiki/Dried_Berry_Pie

Dried Mixed Berry Pie is a food item made by the Dehydrator from Mixed Berry Pie. It doesn't spoil and is inedible until restored at the Rehydrator.
Recipes
Dehydrator: 6000 kcal Mixed Berry Pie + 12 kg Plastic = 6 units Dried Mixed Berry Pie + 6 kg Water
Rehydrator: 1 unit Dried Mixed Berry Pie + 1 kg Water = rehydrated Mixed Berry Pie
History

---

# 文档：Dried Duplicant

- 类别：food
- 标识：dried duplicant
- 来源：wiki/Dried_Duplicant

Dried Duplicant is a item made by the Dehydrator from a Duplicant. The Duplicant will inside will live forever, but is unable to work until restored at the Rehydrator.

Because the Duplicant inside is unable to perform actions, care should be taken to not accidentally dehydrate your last Duplicant, or otherwise have a situation where no Duplicant is remaining to rehydrate them. All living Duplicants being dehydrated will result in a colony failure as though all Duplicants had died.

Given as a dehydrated Duplicant will no longer require constant food or oxygen, this makes dehydrating Duplicants for space travel a viable strategy.

Sending a dehydrated Duplicant into the Temporal Tear will not trigger any of the related events.
Recipes
Dehydrator: 1 unit Duplicant + 25 kg Plastic = 1 unit Dried Duplicant + 6 kg Water
Rehydrator: 1 unit Dried Duplicant + 1 kg Water = rehydrated Duplicant

---

# 文档：Frost Bun

- 类别：food
- 标识：frost bun
- 来源：wiki/Frost_Bun

Frost Bun is a food item made at the Electric Grill from 3 Sleet Wheat Grain It has a Food Quality of Standard (+2) and provides 1200 kcal.

Recipes
Inside the Gas Range, it can be cooked into:
Frost Burger

Tips
6 Frost Bun orders can be made at the Electric Grill every time a Sleet Wheat plant is harvested.
Feeding your Duplicant<nowiki/>s only Frost Buns will require 2.5(domestic)/10(wild) Sleet Wheat plants per dupe.

---

# 文档：Frost Burger

- 类别：food
- 标识：frost burger
- 来源：wiki/Frost_Burger

Frost Burger is a food item made in the Gas Range with 1200kcal Frost Bun, 400kcal Lettuce, and 4000kcal Barbeque each. It has a Food Quality of Ambrosial (+6).

Frost Burger has the highest food quality in the game and gives dupes a unique Soul Food effect, which grants -15% stress relief and -2 Athletics for 2 cycles.

Cooking and serving Frost Burgers is usually not worth it, because only dupes with the Gourmet trait will gain additional morale bonus and the lengthy -2 Athletics penalty is quite negative. However, feeding burgers to especially stressed dupes might help soothe them.

For long-time storage it can be kept in  environment while being  or be dehydrated.
History

---

# 文档：Gristle Berry

- 类别：food
- 标识：gristle berry
- 来源：wiki/Gristle_Berry

Gristle Berry is a food item made at the Electric Grill from 1600 kcal Bristle Berry (1 Bristle Blossom). It has a Food Quality of Poor(+1) and provides 2000 kcal.

Recipes
The Gas Range can cook 2000 kcal  with 1000kcal Grubfruit and 3  into 4200 kcal
4000kcal of  can be cooked with 2kg of  to produce 4400

Tips
When turning Bristle Berry into Gristle Berry you gain a 400 kcal increase. This decreases the number of Bristle Blossoms you need from 3.75(domestic)/15(wild) to 3(domestic)/12(wild) per dupe.

Grubfruits are the fruit of the non-Spindly Grubfruit Plants. they have the lowest calorie density of any food in the game.

# 文档：Grubfruit Preserve

- 类别：food
- 标识：grubfruit preserve
- 来源：wiki/Grubfruit_Preserve

Grubfruit Preserve is a food item made from 8  (2000 kcal) and 4kg . It has a Food Quality of  and provides 2400 kcal. Grubfruit Preserves, together with , boast the second highest shelf life possible at 32 cycles, only outclassed by  Berry Sludge (which has the same quality), but the Preserves have much higher Quality than Pickled Meal.

There are no recipes using Grubfruit Preserve as an ingredient to create more sophisticated food.

# 文档：Lettuce

- 类别：food
- 标识：lettuce
- 来源：wiki/Lettuce

Lettuce is a food item grown from Waterweed in 12 kg per harvest which is equivalent to 4800 kcal. It has a Food Quality of Terrible (0).

Recipes
Inside the Gas Range, it can be cooked into :
1600 kcal per Mushroom Wrap recipe,
400 kcal per Mushroom Quiche recipe,
400 kcal per Frost Burger recipe.

Tips
12 Frost Burger orders can be made for each growth cycle of Waterweed. This means if you choose to feed your Duplicants only Frost Burgers you will need ~0.166(domestic)/~0.666(wild) Waterweed plants per duplicant to supply the Lettuce.
3 Mushroom Wraps can be made for each growth cycle of Waterweed. This means if you choose to feed your Duplicants only Mushroom Wraps you will need ~0.833(domestic)/~3.333(wild) Waterweed plants per duplicant to supply the Lettuce.

---

# 文档：Liceloaf

- 类别：food
- 标识：liceloaf
- 来源：wiki/Liceloaf

Liceloaf can spread Food Poisoning if Water used to create it was contaminated with germs.

Tips
Making Liceloaf effectively converts 50 kg of water into 500 kcal of food, which is somewhat less efficient than Bristle Blossom farming, which can convert 50 kg of water into 833.3 kcal of Gristle Berry. If water is in a limited supply and Dirt is plentiful, the Meal Lice should probably be eaten raw.
The process to make Liceloaf is also rather long - but it does not require the Cooking skill.

---

# 文档：Meal Lice

- 类别：food
- 标识：meal lice
- 来源：wiki/Meal_Lice

Meal Lice is one of the worst Food Quality. However, Mealwood plants are economic to grow, as they require only dirt (10kg/cycle) and no water. This makes Mealwood especially useful in dry starts, such as Forest Biome.

A Juicer requires 250g Meal Lice per use as one of its ingredients.

Recipes
It can be processed in a Microbe Musher to create Liceloaf or an Electric Grill to make Pickled Meal.

Tips
Cooking Meal Lice into Liceloaf produces fewer additional kcal, and with lower quality, than making Gristle Berry with the same water, Consequently, Meal Lice is generally better eaten raw or turned into Pickled Meal.
Feeding Dreckos with Meal Lice increases the chance to get a Glossy Drecko egg.

# 文档：Mixed Berry Pie

- 类别：food
- 标识：mixed berry pie
- 来源：wiki/Mixed_Berry_Pie

Mixed Berry Pie is a late-game food added in the Spaced Out! DLC, requiring Duplicants to combine Grubfruits, Bristle Berries and Sleet Wheat in a Gas Range to cook. Bristle Berries must be cooked into Gristle Berries on an Electric Grill first. Cooking  in this way nets no additional calories for your dupes, but it does increase Food Quality to .

Mixed Berry Pie is one of two Superb foods that do not require Pincha Pepper to produce, simplifying the temperature ranges required for your farm plots somewhat and removing the need for Polluted Water.

For long-time storage it can be kept in  environment while being  or be dehydrated.
History

---

# 文档：Muckroot

- 类别：food
- 标识：muckroot
- 来源：wiki/Muckroot

Muckroot is a non-renewable Food item. It can be gathered either by uprooting a Buried Muckroot, or occasionally when unearthing Buried Objects in the Temperate Biome.

Muckroots can only be consumed directly; there are no recipes using them as an ingredient.

They also never spoil, and cannot be broken down in the compost pile.

History

---

# 文档：Mush Bar

- 类别：food
- 标识：mush bar
- 来源：wiki/Mush_Bar

The Mush Bar is a food item made using the Microbe Musher. It provides 800 kcal/kg and has a Food Quality of Grisly (-1). It requires Dirt, Water, and Power to produce it, and a Duplicant doing the Cook errand.

Mush Bar are created with at least 1000 Food Poisoning germs even if the Water and Dirt used to create it were free of germs. The germs are eliminated most effectively by frying Mush Bar in an Electric Grill to make a Mush Fry. Ensure hand washing facilities are available to avoid immediately re-infecting the Mush Fry.

Mush bars are highly recommended for all colonies, especially new players. They can and should serve as a primary food source for the entire game.

Version History
Mush Bar previously had a chance to induce Diarrhea, this was replaced with 1000 Food Poisoning germs.

---

# 文档：Mush Fry

- 类别：food
- 标识：mush fry
- 来源：wiki/Mush_Fry

The Mush Fry is a food item made from 800 kcal of Mush Bar. It has a Food Quality of 0 and provides 1,050 kcal.

There are no recipes using Mush Fry as an ingredient to create more sophisticated food.

Tips
Mush Frys allow you to feed your Duplicants for ~71.4 kg Dirt and ~71.4 kg Water<nowiki/> per cycle
Do everything in your power to avoid making Mush Bars and always turn the ones you have into Mush Frys!

---

# 文档：Mushroom

- 类别：food
- 标识：mushroom
- 来源：wiki/Mushroom

Mushroom is a produce harvested from Dusk Cap.

Recipes
Mushrooms can be cooked into Fried Mushroom with Electric Grill.
Mushrooms also consumed in Juicer to augment morale and strength attribute.

Requirements
Dusk Caps require Slime and a Carbon Dioxide environment to produce Mushrooms.

Mass
The mass of a single Mushroom (2400 kcal) is 1000g.

Stats for 1000 kcal of Mushroom
1000 kcal are produced in 3.125 Cycles (and 320 kcal are produced by each Cycle).
1000 kcal of Mushroom weigh 0.416 kg.
12.5 kg of Slime are necessary to produce 1000 kcal of Mushroom.

History

---

# 文档：Mushroom Quiche

- 类别：food
- 标识：mushroom quiche
- 来源：wiki/Mushroom_Quiche

Mushroom Quiche is a food item made with 2800 kcal Omelette, 400 kcal Lettuce, and 2800 kcal Fried Mushroom at the Gas Range. It has a Food Quality of +5 and provides 6400 kcal.

It is currently the highest kcal-to-kg holder and the only Superb quality food that gives the buff "Radiation Resistant: Aquatic Diet."

History

---

# 文档：Mushroom Wrap

- 类别：food
- 标识：mushroom wrap
- 来源：wiki/Mushroom_Wrap

Mushroom Wrap is a food item made with Fried Mushroom and Lettuce at the Gas Range. It provides 4,800 kcal with food quality of .

Assuming all plants are properly tended to and harvested on time, feeding your Duplicants Mushroom Wrap indefinitely will require 1.5625 Dusk Cap plants per duplicant and 0.8333 Waterweed Plants per duplicant.

There are no recipes using Mushroom Wrap as an ingredient to create even more sophisticated food.

For long-time storage it can be kept in  environment while being  or be dehydrated.

Tips
Mushroom Quiche can be considered an upgrade as it requires the same ingredients + Omelette and has a higher food quality

History

# 文档：Nosh Bean

- 类别：food
- 标识：nosh bean
- 来源：wiki/Nosh_Bean

The Nosh Bean is both seed and product of Nosh Sprout.

How to obtain
It can be obtained by harvesting and uprooting Nosh Sprout or by digging up Buried Objects within a Rust Biome.

There is no way to gain Nosh Beans if the chosen Asteroid Type has no Rust Biome or to regain them after every Nosh Bean spoiled. For long-time storage Nosh Bean can be kept in  environment while being  or be .

Usage
Seed
Nosh Bean can be planted in Planter Boxes, Farm Tiles, and Hydroponic Farms. When the plant reaches maturity 12 Nosh Bean can be harvested.

Critter Food
Since the February 2024 QoL Update, Pacu can eat 1 Unit/cycle.

Recipes
As a food ingredient it is unedible while raw, but can be cooked into various foods or crushed into Brackene.

# 文档：Nutrient Bar

- 类别：food
- 标识：nutrient bar
- 来源：wiki/Nutrient_Bar

Nutrient Bars are food items. The Ration Box at the start of the game contains 20 kg (16000 kcal) of Nutrient Bars.

Nutrient Bars cannot be made by Duplicants, but the Printing Pod can also sometimes offer more Nutrient Bars as a care package. 1 kg of Nutrient Bars also can be found in Vending Machines by rummaging inside it.

Nutrient Bars never spoil.

Nutrient Bars can only be consumed directly, there are no recipes using them as an ingredient.

Trivia
The Nutrient Bar used to be called 'Field Ration'.

---

# 文档：Omelette

- 类别：food
- 标识：omelette
- 来源：wiki/Omelette

The Omelette is a food item made from 1,600 kcals of Raw Egg, when cooked in the Electric Grill, or when a Raw Egg is heated to 70°C. It has a Food Quality of 2 and provides 2,800 kcals.

Omelettes can be used to cook Mushroom Quiche in the Gas Range.

Tips
Since Omelettes can be cooked by heating raw egg, they can be moved into a heated area by Conveyor Rails and Auto-Sweepers to make food with minimal dupe labor.

---

# 文档：Pepper Bread

- 类别：food
- 标识：pepper bread
- 来源：wiki/Pepper_Bread

Pepper Bread is a food item made from 10 Sleet Wheat Grain and 1 Pincha Peppernut at the Gas Range. It has a Food Quality of Superb (+5) and provides 4,000 kcal.

Calorie-wise Pepper Bread is mostly equivalent to Frost Buns, albeit slightly more expensive in its resource cost. Compared to the Frost Burger, it may be preferable to cook Sleet Wheat into Pepper Bread, since they both provide the same morale bonus to duplicants without the Gourmet trait and Pepper Bread does not carry a penalty to the Athletics skill.

Feeding your Duplicants Pepper Bread indefinitely will require 2.5/10 (domestic/wild) Sleet Wheat plants and 0.5/2 (domestic/wild) Pincha Pepper Plants per duplicant, assuming the plants are harvested by a dupe.

There are no recipes using Pepper Bread as an ingredient to create even more sophisticated food.

For long-time storage it can be kept in  environment while being  or be dehydrated.

History

---

# 文档：Pickled Meal

- 类别：food
- 标识：pickled meal
- 来源：wiki/Pickled_Meal

Pickled Meal is a food item made from 3 Meal Lice (1800 kcal). It has a Food Quality of -1 (Grisly) and provides 1800 kcal. Pickled Meal (and Grubfruit Preserve) have the highest shelf life possible (besides the items with unlimited shelf life). Since it is cooked at an Electric Grill, any food poisoning germs present on the ingredients (meal lice) will not survive.

There are no recipes using Pickled Meal as an ingredient to create more sophisticated food.

Tips
Meal lice gains 500 calories when turned into Liceloaf for 50 kg water versus having the same amount calories when turned into Pickled Meal.
One side-effect of not using water for meal preparation, is that your dupes will not get sick from germy water.
Pickled Meal has a very peculiar effect in that it is the only cooked food to destroy Food Poisoning germs in room temperature, meaning that it eliminates most of the risk of food poisoning, even if a dupe has not washed up recently.

---

# 文档：Pincha Peppernut

- 类别：food
- 标识：pincha peppernut
- 来源：wiki/Pincha_Peppernut

Pincha Peppernuts are grown and can be harvested from the Pincha Pepper Plant. Pincha Peppernuts are very useful in the creation of late game foods, such as Pepper Bread, Stuffed Berry, and Spicy Tofu.

Food
All Pincha Peppernut recipes are made at the Gas Range. A domestic Pincha Pepper produces 4 kg of Pincha Peppernuts every 8 cycles, an average of 500 g/cycle.

# 文档：Raw Egg

- 类别：food
- 标识：raw egg
- 来源：wiki/Raw_Egg

Raw Egg can be made from an Egg using an Egg Cracker. It is edible, but it is better to prepare it on Electric Grill or Gas Range.  Raw Egg will turn into Omelette if exposed to a hot temperature for an extended time

Eggs stored in Storage Bins and other containers lose viability over time and will become a Raw Egg in 10 cycles if not released from the container.

Tips
A Raw Egg will cook into an omelette if it reaches 71°C.
As cracking doesn't change the temperature, cracking an egg of 71°C or higher produces an Omelette.
If an egg reaches 0% viability in a container and becomes a Raw Egg, its temperature is reset to 20°C.

Recipes
Inside the Electric Grill, it can be cooked into
Omelette
Soufflé Pancakes

History

---

# 文档：Sleet Wheat Grain

- 类别：food
- 标识：sleet wheat grain
- 来源：wiki/Sleet_Wheat_Grain

Sleet Wheat Grain is produced by Sleet Wheat every 18 Cycles. Harvesting Sleet Wheat yields 18 Sleet Wheat Grains.  Sleet Wheat is inedible when unprepared.

Unlike all other foods and ingredients, Sleet Wheat Grain is Deep Frozen below 10°C and Refrigerated below 35°C. If it is frozen and in a sterile gas, it will be preserved indefinitely. However, if it is in oxygen or polluted oxygen it will decay at -3%  and -6% per cycle respectively. Therefore, when harvesting the wild sleet wheat found in the frozen biome, it is desirable to extract all the oxygen and polluted oxygen to ensure the grain does not rot. This is a good strategy in the early game to ensure a constant supply of sleet wheat grain.

Plants
Each Sleet Wheat Grain can be planted to grow a new plant and should only be planted in a sub-zero environment as well as supplied with nearly freezing water due to requiring an internal temperature of 5°C or less to grow.

- 类别：food
- 标识：soufflé pancakes
- 来源：wiki/Soufflé_Pancakes

Soufflé Pancakes are prepared at an Electric Grill with 1600 kcal worth of Raw Egg and 2 Sleet Wheat Grain. It provides 3600 kcal with food quality of Good (+3).

There are no recipes using Soufflé Pancakes as an ingredient to create more sophisticated food.

Tips
9 Soufflé Pancakes can be made every time a Sleet Wheat plant is harvested.
Feeding your Duplicant<nowiki/>s only Soufflé Pancakes will require 0.56(domestic)/2.24(wild) Sleet Wheat plants per dupe, and 444 kcal of egg per dupe.

# 文档：Spindly Grubfruit

- 类别：food
- 标识：spindly grubfruit
- 来源：wiki/Spindly_Grubfruit

A Grubfruit that failed to develop properly.
It is nonetheless edible, and vaguely tasty. It provides 800 kcal per fruit (one fruit is 1kg) and its Food Quality is . It can be cooked in the Electric Grill to make Roast Grubfruit Nut, increasing its calories count to 1200kcal.

- 标识：swamp chard heart
- 来源：wiki/Swamp_Chard_Heart

Swamp Chard Heart a non-renewable Food, just like Muckroot and Hexalent. It's an early-game source of kilo-calories before the player establishes some form of food production, like a farm.

Swamp Chard Heart may be gathered by uprooting a Swamp Chard which is found in Swampy Biome.

It can only be consumed directly, there are no recipes with it.

## GASES

# 文档：Atmospheric Pressure

- 类别：gases
- 标识：atmospheric pressure
- 来源：wiki/Atmospheric_Pressure

Atmospheric Pressure  is based on the amount, mass, and type of gas filling a space at a time.

If two gases interact, the gas with the most pressure will force the other gas out of its area (mostly seen between  and ).

Effects
On Duplicants
The Breathability of  and  is dependant on the the Atmospheric Pressure.
+
Atmospheric Pressure|| Breathability || Effects
above 1 kg || Very breathable
525 g to 1 kg || Breathable
50 g to 525 g || Barely Breathable || Duplicants will get the +10% Stress/Cycle due to Low Oxygen for the duration they remain in a Low Oxygen environment.
below 50 g || Unbreathable || Duplicants will hold their breath, but will not suffer from a Low Oxygen debuff
Additionally, if the Atmospheric Pressure of any Gas a Duplicant is inside is above 4 kg, Duplicants will get Popped Eardrums, a +20% Stress/cycle debuff that lasts for half a cycle.

On Plants
Most Plants can only grow if enough, but not too much Atmospheric Pressure is present. This is most often the range from 150 g to 10 kg, but Nosh Sprout, Dasha Saltvine, and Oxyfern go as low as 10g, and Waterweed can be submerged in up to 950 kg of liquid. Single use consumable plants, such as Muckroot don't need any specific Atmospheric Pressure, and neither do Wheezewort, Thimble Reed, nor Jumping Joya.

On Machinery
Machines whose main purpose is to generate gasses such as the Electrolyzer and Oxygen Diffuser will stop running and give an overpressure warning at 1.8kg. While a Petroleum Generator which produces  as a side product, does not.

On Geysers
Geysers, Vents, and Volcanoes also can be forced to stop erupting once they are over-pressured.
150 kg overpressure Volcanoes, Minor Volcanoes and Metal Volcanoes
500 kg overpressure Water Geysers/Vents (Polluted, Cool Slush, Salt, and Cool Salt Slush)
5kg overpressure Gas Vents (Carbon Dioxide, Hydrogen, Hot Polluted Oxygen and Infectious Polluted Oxygen, Chlorine, and Natural Gas)

On Emitting Elements
Offgassing Elements such as Oxylite or Polluted Water will stop producing emitting their respective element at 1,800 grams Atmospheric Pressure.

---

These gases will allow Duplicants to breathe.

Oxygen
Polluted Oxygen

# 文档：Carbon Dioxide

- 类别：gases
- 标识：carbon dioxide
- 来源：wiki/Carbon_Dioxide

Carbon Dioxide is a common gas resource. It is exhaled by Duplicants and occurs naturally in almost all Biomes. It is heavier than most other gases and will sink to the lowest elevation if lighter gases are present.

Usage
Carbon Dioxide is considered sterile and in large concentrations will prevent food rot if the food is also kept frozen. Due to ease of handling (tendency to pool in pits) and acquisition (funnel-shaped bases will have a large pool of it at the bottom), it is easily harvested for food storage solutions.
Dusk Caps and Oxyferns require Carbon Dioxide atmosphere to grow.
Slicksters breathe Carbon Dioxide and excrete Crude Oil.
Molten Slicksters breathe Carbon Dioxide and excrete Petroleum.
Carbon Dioxide can be 'captured' into Polluted Water by:
Algae Terrariums, at rate of 333.33 mg/s or 200 g/cycle while costing 300g/s of Water and producing 290.33g/s of Polluted Water
Carbon Skimmers, at rate of 300 g/s, or 180 kg/cycle while converting 1kg/s of Water into 1kg/s of Polluted Water
Soda Fountain consumes 5 kg of Water and 1 kg of Carbon Dioxide per use. It grants +4 Morale and +1 Science to Duplicants.
Beeta will consume 100 g / s of Carbon Dioxide. This causes them to fall asleep, preventing them from stinging Duplicants. A sleeping Beeta produces 1416 rads/cycle of radiation.

Production
Duplicants breathe out 2 g/s of Carbon Dioxide, or 1.2 kg/cycle.
Polymer Presses produce Carbon Dioxide at rate of 8.33 g/s, or 5 kg/cycle.
Gas Range: 25 g/s, or 15 kg/cycle.
Ethanol Distillers: 166.67 g/s, or 100 kg/cycle.
Carbon-burning generators output Carbon Dioxide as a by-product:
scope="col" | Output
(g/sec)
scope="col" | Output
(kg/cycle)
scope="col" | Power / CO2 Mass
(W/g)
Coal Generator       || 20.0|| 12.0||30.00
Natural Gas Generator|| 22.5|| 13.5||35.56
Wood Burner          ||170.0||102.0|| 1.76
Petroleum Generator  ||500.0||300.0|| 4.00
There are two types of Geysers that produce Carbon Dioxide with varying rates:
Carbon Dioxide Vents, which produce ~100 g/s at 500 °C, which is too hot even for Slicksters.
Liquid Carbon Dioxide Geysers, which produce ~150 g/s at -55 °C, those are more immediately usable and can be passed along industrial sections to cool them down.
Rocket's Petroleum Engines and Solid Fuel Thrusters exhausts superheated Carbon Dioxide.
Meteor Showers bring some Carbon Dioxide with them.
It can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Forested Ore Fields at a rate of 108 – 324 kg per cycle.
In Radioactive Gas Clouds at a rate of 31.8 – 127.2 kg per cycle.
In Glimmering Asteroid Fields at a rate of 30 – 90 kg per cycle.
5 other types of POIs produce Solid Carbon Dioxide.

Tips
If cooled below condensation temperature, it can safely be stored away as a liquid or solid.
Despite creating a  sterile environment, Carbon Dioxide does not prevent Compost from working and is perfectly safe for plants. The tendency to pool at the bottom can help to ensure adequate air pressure.
In early game, to prevent CO2 buildups, many players build 'Carbon pits', where they pool carbon dioxide until they are able to get rid of it with Carbon Skimmers, compress it,  vent it into space or otherwise deal with it.

Trivia
Under regular atmospheric conditions, real-life Carbon Dioxide actually bypasses the liquid phase entirely. Only above a pressure of 518 kPa, about five times standard atmospheric pressure, does liquid Carbon Dioxide actually form. However, ONI does not simulate the influence of pressure on phase transitions, and includes liquid Carbon Dioxide.

---

# 文档：Chlorine

- 类别：gases
- 标识：chlorine
- 来源：wiki/Chlorine

Chlorine is a gas found naturally occurring in the map. It is the second highest density gas after Carbon Dioxide at the same temperature. Chlorine is a great deterrent against germs, and the best possible heat insulator among gases.

Chlorine is deadly to all germs including Food Poisoning and Slimelung. Surrounding any storage building with chlorine for a full cycle is a sure way to totally disinfect all contents of said building. A Duplicant traveling through Chlorine will not be cured of any diseases, but the surface germs on them will be subjected to the toxic gas.

As of version EX1-449549 onwards, Duplicants moving through Chlorine Gas for more than three seconds will be hit by the Eye Irritation debuff, which reduces Athletics.

Production
Chlorine is a renewable resource, produced by the Chlorine Gas Vent.
Bleach Stone in its item state emits Chlorine unless pressurized (for example, by water).
The Rust Deoxidizer produces chlorine along with its other outputs.
The Gas can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Chlorine Clouds at a rate of 135 – 405 kg per cycle.
In Radioactive Gas Clouds at a rate of 9.1 – 36.4 kg per cycle.
The liquid can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Chlorine Cloud at a rate of 135 - 405 kg per cycle.
In Radioactive Gas Cloud at a rate of 9.1 - 36.4 kg per cycle.

Due to relatively high condensation point of Chlorine gas, small amounts of Liquid Chlorine can be encountered naturally in the Frozen Biome, where temperatures can reach -40 °C. Chlorine is notable for its very low thermal capacity and conductivity, and liquid state at low temperature.

Usage
A Chlorine gas room is great at disinfection and heat insulation.
Contact with Chlorine gas will quickly kill all germs from the contents of machines and storage buildings. However, it is important to note that it will not remove germs from contents of pipes.
It is good for germy slime storage and processing (or any items you want to disinfect). Just remember that it takes a full cycle to destroy all germs.
While not perfect, it also can serve as early, more-resilient alternative to the Vacuum chamber.
As an insulator it is slightly worse than Insulated Tile made of Ceramic, however its low density makes it a poor buffer even when pressurized.
Chlorine is consumed when disinfecting objects. This results in mass deletion of Chlorine when coming into contact with the morbillion germs Morbius Crohn inflicts on Duplicants.
The Ore Scrubber removes germs from objects and it is a way to use chlorine. However, it needs a duplicant operator, who also needs to handle the infected goods.
The Balm Lily needs to be surrounded by chlorine and does not need any care at all. It has good synergy with Stable of Dreckos, generating infinite renewable Phosphorite.
Balm Lily Flower and Phosphorite dropped by Dreckos, used together produce Medical Pack, which heals Slimelung.
Dasha Saltvine requires Chlorine atmosphere and consumes small amounts of it (6 g/s, or 3.6 kg/cycle).
Gas Grass consumes liquid Chlorine (500 g/cycle).
Puft Princes and Squeaky Pufts can breathe Chlorine and excrete Bleach Stone, which is consumed by Hand Sanitizers, Hot Tubs, Waterweed, and Geotuners.
Failing to use excess of Chlorine, you can always pump it out into the void of Space.
Gas Grass requires 500 grams of Liquid Chlorine irrigation per cycle.

Misconceptions
Chlorine does not directly harm dupes any more than the slowness from Eye Irritation or other non-breathable gases, and does not cause permanent damage.

Gallery

---

# 文档：Ethanol

- 类别：gases
- 标识：ethanol
- 来源：wiki/Ethanol

Ethanol is a liquid fuel refined from Lumber. It also appears naturally in Rust Biome. It can be used as a Power source.

Usage
Petroleum Generator can burn Ethanol or Petroleum to generate power:
2 kg/s Ethanol or Petroleum = 2 kW Power + 500 g/s Carbon Dioxide + 750 g/s Polluted Water
Nosh Sprout domestic growth requires 20 kg/cycle Ethanol irrigation.
Ethanol has decent Heat Capacity and very low freezing point (-114ºC), making it probably the best mid-game (pre-Super Coolant) freezer coolant, that can often be found laying around the map.** It should be noted that Ethanol has a considerably lower Specific Heat Capacity compared to water-based liquids, so more energy must be spent to cool it per degree than water, leading to electricity waste unless the lower freezing temperature is a factor. Still, it's 12% more power-efficient than Naphtha, 40% better than Petroleum, 46% better than Crude Oil, and (after accounting for the differences between a Thermo Aquatuner and Thermo Regulator), more than twice as efficient as Hydrogen.
It's less efficient than Polluted Water, but that leaves you very little room for error between the required -18ºC threshold for Deep Freeze and its freezing point, -20.6ºC. Brine is slightly more forgiving, but much harder to acquire.
Ethanol has decent Heat Capacity, very low Heat Conductivity, and 192 degrees range, making it a decent liquid insulator, although mostly in the lower temperature range.
However, once Ethanol is turned into gas at 80 °C its heat parameters while slightly lower are comparable to Hydrogen, which makes Ethanol gas quite decent heat transfer agent at above 100 °C temperatures.
Due to the specific heat capacity difference between the liquid and gas, repeatedly boiling and condensing ethanol can serve as a heat deletion method.
Its thermal properties make it best for maintaining sub-zero temperatures for Sleet Wheat farms, with Radiant Liquid Piping compensating for their low conductivity. Furthermore, the low thermal conductivity makes mopping up easier, in the case of accidents.
Assuming the wood is acquired from a domestic Arbor Tree, the Ethanol Distiller converts 1 kg of Polluted Water into 2.4 kg of Ethanol. A Petroleum Generator converts Ethanol at 37.5% ratio, or 2.4 kg of Ethanol into 0.9 kg of Polluted Water.

Production
Ethanol Distiller can produce Ethanol from Lumber:
1 kg/s Lumber = 500 g/s Ethanol + 333.33 g/s Polluted Dirt + 166.67 g/s Carbon Dioxide.

Reference

---

# 文档：Gas

- 类别：gases
- 标识：gas
- 来源：wiki/Gas

Gases are substances that expand to fill their container.

coal
Mechanics
will condense into a liquid if cooled 3 °C under their condensation point. The same, liquids will evaporate if heated up 3 °C above their condensation point.
Unlike liquids, gases will always spread to nearby vacuum tiles (unless less than 1 microgram of the gas is present).
Elements with a lower density tend to rise above others. In the case of gases with the same density (e.g. Oxygen and Polluted Oxygen), they tend to group together and form different layers.
There are heat convection mechanics. The heated gasses will rise upwards, while the colder gasses will be pushed down, the gasses with similar temperatures tend to semi-randomly spread horizontally.
Duplicants can breathe Oxygen and Polluted Oxygen.
Unless specified, Critters do not breathe, and may survive in any gas as long as other conditions are met.
They can also survive in a vacuum.
Airborn Critters can fly/float in a vacuum.
will be destroyed when exposed to space, unless protected by Drywall.
can be stored in a Gas Reservoir.
Duplicants can be scalded by hot Gases like Steam. Wearing an Atmo Suit will protect them.

List of Gases
Gases tend to stratify (separate by height) as follows, from lightest to heaviest:

Trivia
Real-life oxygen has a "density" (molecular mass) of about 32 g/mol, as in "natural" state it forms two atom (of 16 mass each) particles.

# 文档：Hydrogen

- 类别：gases
- 标识：hydrogen
- 来源：wiki/Hydrogen

Hydrogen Gas is one of the Resources in the game Oxygen Not Included. It is an unbreathable Gas that is extremely light and will rise above all other gases. This means that it will settle at the top of rooms and other open areas.

Hydrogen can easily be density-separated with a reverse funnel at the top of your base, and collected with a pump when levels get too high.

Production
Hydrogen can be found naturally in small quantities in the Caustic and Tide Pool Biome.
It is produced alongside Oxygen in an Electrolyzer using water and electricity
Hydrogen Vents produce Hydrogen at various rates during their active states.
Plug Slugs will produce Hydrogen after consuming metal ores (3kg/cycle/critter).
It can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Exploded Gas Giants at a rate of 105 – 280 kg per cycle.
In Helium Clouds at a rate of 60 – 180 kg per cycle.

Usage
In the current build of the game, Hydrogen has several uses:
It can be burned in the Hydrogen Generator to produce 800 W of power. See Hydrogen Generator#Practicality.
It can be condensed into Liquid Hydrogen to serve as a rocket fuel for Hydrogen Engine, the most powerful type of rocket-engine. Condensation of Hydrogen requires a dedicated cooling setup using the most advanced materials.
It can be stockpiled and utilized as heat transfer agent due to its high thermal parameters.
Dreckos and Glossy Dreckos require spending time in Hydrogen atmosphere to grow their scales of Reed Fiber or Plastic.
It is one of the best gasses to use with the Thermo Regulator because of its high Specific Heat Capacity, high Thermal Conductivity and the fact that remains in the gas state until extremely low temperatures. That said, for most heat transfer applications the Thermo Aquatuner is more practical.
Extreme temperatures, where most liquids would boil, would make the use of Hydrogen as a working fluid practical - as do low temperatures where most liquids would freeze. In particular, it can be used instead of Super Coolant in the processing of Sour Gas or production of Liquid Oxygen.
With the use of Radiant Gas Piping and how Thermal Conductivity works, Hydrogen's low thermal conductivity compared to liquids is not as much of an issue as it appears - however, the solid materials involved still heavily favor Radiant Liquid Piping, as even Aluminum Ore has only a fraction of the thermal conductivity of any Refined Metal. The exception is Steel and Thermium gas pipes, which have the same thermal conductivity as their liquid counterparts but use half as much metal to build.

Cooling
Hydrogen can be used to power the Anti Entropy Thermo-Nullifier, which produces -80 kDTU/s at the cost of only 10 g/s of Hydrogen. Venting extra hydrogen into the cold biome and then back, or using natural convection, will quickly cool your base.

Locking Wheezeworts in a room with a Hydrogen atmosphere, increases their cooling efficiency.

Thermo Regulators can be put in the same room, it will prevent them from overheating, while they are used to cool other gases in your base (like your oxygen).

More power-efficient setup, that generates consistent, controlled temperature, will include Mechanized Airlock paired with Thermo Sensor and oil/metal buffer.

Gallery

---

# 文档：Natural Gas

- 类别：gases
- 标识：natural gas
- 来源：wiki/Natural_Gas

Natural Gas is an unbreathable, relatively heavy gas, which sinks below Oxygen but rises above Chlorine and Carbon Dioxide.

Usage
Natural gas is burned in the Natural Gas Generator. The generator consumes 90 g/s Natural Gas, and generates 800 W Power, 67.5 g/s Polluted Water, and 22.5 g/s Carbon Dioxide.
Natural gas is consumed by Gas Range to produce food of the highest quality.

Production
Natural Gas Geysers are the main source of Natural Gas.
Oil Refinery produces 90 g/s Natural Gas by refining Crude Oil to Petroleum.
Oil Well produces 33.3 g/s of Natural Gas alongside Crude Oil.
Condensing Sour Gas produced from Petroleum yields Methane at a 2/3 mass ratio. Methane vaporizes to Natural Gas.
Gassy Moos can eat Gas Grass and excrete Natural Gas (16.65 g/s).
Fertilizer Synthesizer emits 10 g/s Natural Gas as a by-product.
Duplicants with the Flatulent trait emit 100g of Natural Gas every 10-40 seconds. (10-2.5 g/s)
Turning it from mild annoyance into sustainable energy source will require at least 9 flatulent dupes, and 36 will be able to supply one generator continuously (with 3 more generators used as an overflow). This is without counting energy spent on necessary air filtering.
It can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Exploded Gas Giants at a rate of 45 – 120 kg per cycle, as a solid, liquid and gas.
In Exploded Ice Giants at a rate of 27 – 81 kg per cycle, as a solid.
In Oily Asteroid Fields at a rate of 17 – 56.5 kg per cycle, as a solid.

---

# 文档：Oxygen

- 类别：gases
- 标识：oxygen
- 来源：wiki/Oxygen

Oxygen is one of the Resources in the game Oxygen Not Included. It is a Breathable Gas and required by Duplicants to survive. It can be produced by machines (Oxygen Diffuser, Electrolyzer, Rust Deoxidizer), filtered from Polluted Oxygen by Deodorizers or cooling to liquid form, or a small amount created by the Algae Terrarium.

Mechanics
Oxygen is one of the lightest gases. Oxygen can be breathed in by Duplicants and exhaled as Carbon Dioxide. Due to the fact that Oxygen is lighter than Carbon Dioxide it will rise above it.

Although Duplicants require Oxygen to live, Oxygen is only breathable in high enough quantities (anything below 50 g/tile is unbreathable while anything between 50 and 300 g/tile is breathable but will stress Duplicants).

Duplicants typically use 100 grams of Oxygen per second (200 g/s with Mouth Breather trait, 75 g/s with Diver's Lungs, 50 g/s with Deeper Diver's Lungs, and 25 g/s with both). If the pressure is high enough they breathe normally, if it is non-breathable they will hold their breath until breath meter reaches 50%, then stop any task and run to closest spot to refill their lungs. If their breath meter reaches zero, they suffocate to death.

Usage
Atmo Suit, Jet Suit, Oxygen Mask, and Lead Suit Docks require Oxygen to (re)fill their respective suits.
The Telescope requires Oxygen to work.
The Oxylite Refinery produces Oxylite from Oxygen and Gold. 600 g/s Oxygen + 3 g/s Gold = 600 g/s Oxylite.
Puft Princes and Dense Pufts can breathe Oxygen and excrete Oxylite.
Longhair Slicksters consume 30 kg/cycle. and provide some mobile Decor.
When cooled down to liquid state, Liquid Oxygen is a better rocket oxidizer that can be used by Petroleum Engine and Hydrogen Engine.
Although Oxygen has properties that are subpar for fast heat exchanges, applications requiring slow heat exchanges are best performed with Oxygen flowing through a circuit, with Radiant piping at the heat source and the heat sink. For example, maintaining the temperature of the Hydrogen in the Ranch for Dreckos can be done by channelling a dedicated circuit through the Ranch with the heat sink being a cold biome; thus, the ranch will not need cooling via objects that may take up foreground space, e.g. Wheezeworts.
The main advantage of using Oxygen is that the Oxygen can just mix with any Oxygen that is outside the circuit if there is any maintenance or modification that has to be done to the piping while Oxygen is still in it.
Oxygen is also much more available than other gases.

Production
Natural Oxylite emits Oxygen. 5 tiles of Oxylite are guaranteed near the Printing Pod to provide Oxygen for the first few cycles.
Oxygen Diffusers produce Oxygen from Algae. Although this may seem efficient at the start, as the game progresses there is not as much Algae to use.
Electrolyzers produce Oxygen from Water. 1 kg/s Water = 888 g/s Oxygen + 112 g/s Hydrogen. The Hydrogen needs proper handling otherwise it will make the air unbreathable.
Rust Deoxidizer can produce Oxygen, Chlorine and Iron Ore from Rust and Salt. 750 g/s Rust + 250 g/s Salt = 570 g/s Oxygen + 30 g/s Chlorine + 400 g/s Iron Ore.
Algae Terrariums produce Oxygen from Water and Algae. They also consume a tiny amount of nearby Carbon Dioxide, if present. They do not require power, but can be made more efficient when near a light source.
Oxyferns produce Oxygen from Carbon Dioxide.
The Deodorizer purifies Polluted Oxygen into Oxygen using Sand or Regolith as a filtration medium.
It can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Exploded Ice Giants at a rate of 81 – 243 kg per cycle, as a gas.
In Ice Asteroid Fields at a rate of 27 – 81 kg per cycle, as a solid.

See also
Resources
Oxylite solid which emits oxygen
Polluted Oxygen - same as oxygen but transmits germs
Carbon Dioxide - gas emitted from duplicants when breathing

Gallery

---

# 文档：Polluted Oxygen

- 类别：gases
- 标识：polluted oxygen
- 来源：wiki/Polluted_Oxygen

Polluted Oxygen is a gas resource. Polluted Oxygen is breathable and works similarly to Oxygen, allowing Duplicants to survive. However, it also acts as the primary vector of transmission for Slimelung germs, and can just as easily spread Food Poisoning germs. Polluted Oxygen can be found in the world naturally in the Swamp Biome.

Breathing too much Polluted Oxygen causes the Yucky Lungs debuff, which increases the air consumption rate and causes coughing

A Polluted Oxygen atmosphere causes Food nearby to rot at a +100% rate (double default speed) . Further Information: Food (Resource).

Polluted Oxygen has the same density as Oxygen. When Polluted Oxygen and Oxygen are mixed, they tend to group with the same element and form gas layers; however, the heights of such layers is random, with neither density nor temperature having any effect.

Polluted Oxygen spawns naturally as part of Swamp Biomes.

Usage
Deodorizers produce Oxygen and Clay from Polluted Oxygen using a Filtration Medium.
Pufts and Puft Princes can breathe Polluted Oxygen and excrete Slime when they do.

Production
Slime, Polluted Dirt, and bottled Polluted Water all emit Polluted Oxygen into the air in environments with <1800g of air pressure. This spreads any germs present on the substance into the air.
Unbottled Polluted Water will also emit germy Polluted Oxygen into the air in environments with <1800g of air pressure. The rate of production is random.
Morbs produce Polluted Oxygen into the air in environments with <1000g of air pressure without any inputs. They also release Polluted Oxygen upon death.
There are two types of geysers that produce Polluted Oxygen – Hot and Infectious Polluted Oxygen Vents. Both yield ~95&nbsp;g/s and are stifled at 5&nbsp;kg of air pressure, with the latter spreading Slimelung germs. Each of them produces enough polluted oxygen to sustain ~5 wild Pufts, or 1-2 tame ones, but the hotter geyser must be cooled first to not kill critters, especially since it is viable for powering Steam Turbines.
It can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Oxygen Rich Asteroid Field at a rate of 30–100 kg per cycle.
In Organic Mass Field at a rate of 54–162 kg per cycle
Sublimation Station can turn 1000g/s Polluted Dirt into 660g/s Polluted Oxygen.

Tips
Polluted Oxygen can be converted to Liquid Oxygen by cooling it down to its condensation point using an installation involving Thermo Regulators, and then reheating it (see Guide/Cleaning Polluted Oxygen for an example).

Trivia
Polluted Oxygen's former name was "Contaminated Oxygen".

See also
Guide/Oxygen
Guide/Cleaning Polluted Oxygen

---

# 文档：Rock Gas

- 类别：gases
- 标识：rock gas
- 来源：wiki/Rock_Gas

Rock Gas is created when:

Magma is heated above 2359.85 °C (vaporization point + 3 °C).
Molten Glass is heated above 2359.85 °C (vaporization point + 3 °C).
Liquid Uranium is heated above 4134.9 °C (vaporization point + 3 °C).

---

# 文档：Salt

- 类别：gases
- 标识：salt
- 来源：wiki/Salt

Salt is Consumable Ore found in Tide Pool Biome and Rust Biome. When refined to Table Salt, it can be eaten with meals to increase Duplicant Morale by 1.

Usage
Rust Deoxidizer can produce Oxygen, Chlorine, Iron Ore with Rust and Salt. 750 g/s Rust + 250 g/s Salt = 570 g/s Oxygen + 30 g/s Chlorine + 400 g/s Iron Ore.

Rock Crusher can refine Salt into Table Salt. 100 kg Salt = 5 g Table Salt + 100 kg Sand.

Also it can be used at average rate of 83.3 g/s per Geotuner to boost Geysers to increase Polluted Oxygen or Chlorine production

Salt is used to produce Bleach Stone in the Bleach Stone Hopper.
30 kg salt + 500 g Gold = 10 kg Bleach Stone + 20 kg Sand

Due to the specific heat capacity difference between the liquid and gas, repeatedly boiling and condensing Molten Salt can serve as a heat multiplication method.
Production
Salt is available in Tide Pool Biome and Rust Biome.

Dasha Saltvine produces harvestable Salt by consuming Chlorine gas and Sand.

Desalinator can produce Salt from Salt Water or Brine. 5 kg/s Salt Water = 4650 g/s Water + 350 g/s Salt. 5 kg/s Brine = 3500 g/s Water + 1500 g/s Salt.

Heating Salt Water to 101.69 °C (vaporization point + 2 °C) can produce Steam (93% mass) and Salt (7% mass).

Heating Brine to 104.75 °C (vaporization point + 2 °C) can produce Steam (70% mass) and Salt (30% mass).

It can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Interstellar Oceans at a rate of 37.5 – 125 kg per cycle.

---

# 文档：Sour Gas

- 类别：gases
- 标识：sour gas
- 来源：wiki/Sour_Gas

Sour Gas is an intermediary oil product, that can occasionally be found in the Oil Biome when there is a heat leakage from Volcanic Biome.

Production
Sour gas is produced when  or  is heated to 541.85 °C (vaporization point + 3 °C).

Usage
The only thing that can be done with Sour Gas is to cool it. When cooled to -163.5 °C; 67% of its mass becomes  and 33% becomes . If Methane is reheated it becomes . Due to the extreme nature of the cooling required, Thermo Aquatuners will require at least , so it may be better to ignore Sour Gas until then.

The other options are either: the Anti Entropy Thermo-Nullifier, which still might take some time to reach the target temperature and has to be securely heat-isolated. Or thermo regulators running  as coolant, though this requires an efficient heat exchanger in order to come out with more power than was required to sufficiently cool the sour gas.

Tips
Sour Gas serves as the transition route from Petroleum to Natural Gas.
If Sour Gas at sufficiently low pressure is cooled, 100% of its mass condenses into Methane. The exact pressure necessary for this seems to be around 5 grams or less per tile.
and  can theoretically serve as alternatives for Super Coolant.

Two critters are currently in the files but not in-game:

Name !! Picture !! Description
Volgus || || A skittish mammalian creature. It moves in herds for safety.
Shockworm || || Shockworms are exceptionally aggressive and discharge electrical shocks to stun their prey.

Plants
The files mention several plants that are not obtainable:

Name !! Picture !! Description
Avari Vine || || A rapidly growing, subterranean Plant.
Fervine || || A temperature reactive, subterranean Plant.
Palmera Tree || || A large, chlorine-dwelling Plant that can be grown in farm buildings.
Palmeras grow inedible buds that emit unbreathable hydrogen gas.

# 文档：Water

- 类别：gases
- 标识：water
- 来源：wiki/Water

Overview
Water is one of the most important Resources in the game. Water is necessary for making food and supplying Oxygen, but does not need to be directly consumed by Duplicants for survival, contrary to its description. Water has numerous applications regardless of its state.

=Water=
Production
Desalinator can turn Salt Water and Brine into Water and Salt.
Filtering Polluted Water using a Water Sieve.
Melting Snow or Ice, or cooling Steam.
Geysers
Cool Steam Vents periodically produce Steam which will quickly condense into Water. Two are each guaranteed to spawn in the Caustic and Swamp Biome.
Water Geysers periodically produce near-boiling Water.
Steam Turbine and Sauna convert Steam into Water upon use.
Duplicants with the Ugly Crier stress response will produce copious amounts of clean water during their mental break.
It can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Helium Clouds at a rate of 240 – 720 kg per cycle.
In Oxygen Rich Asteroid Fields at a rate of 60 – 200 kg per cycle.

Usage
Pitcher Pump bottles water from open water sources to be used in certain buildings.
Farming:
Bristle Blossom domestic growth requires 20 kg/cycle Water irrigation.
Sleet Wheat domestic growth requires 20 kg/cycle Water irrigation.
Oxyfern domestic growth requires 19 kg/cycle Water irrigation.
Microbe Musher:
Mush Bar from Dirt and Water.
75 kg Dirt + 75 kg Water = 800 kcal Mush Bar.
Liceloaf from Meal Lice and Water.
1200 kcal Meal Lice + 50 kg Water = 1700 kcal Liceloaf.
Tofu from Nosh Bean and Water.
6 unit Nosh Bean + 50 kg Water = 3600 kcal Tofu.
Electrolyzers produce Oxygen and Hydrogen from Water.
1 kg/s Water = 888 g/s Oxygen + 112 g/s Hydrogen.
Algae Terrariums produce Oxygen from Algae and Water.
30 g/s Algae + 300 g/s Water = 40 g/s Oxygen + 290.33 g/s Polluted Water.
If placed in a Carbon Dioxide atmosphere, it can also remove 333.33 mg/s Carbon Dioxide.
Super Computer requires Water for Advanced Research points. Each Advanced Research Point costs 50 kg Water (which must be collected and delivered via bottling).
This cost is certain; improving the efficiency of research, e.g. speeding it up with illumination or having a Duplicant with high Science attribute, will not change it. Rather, having this Research happen faster also accelerates the consumption of Water.
Recreational:
Water Cooler - Each use consumes 1 kg Water and grants +1 Duplicant#Morale to Duplicants.
Espresso Machine - Each use consumes 1 kg Water, 1 kg Pincha Peppernut and grants +4 Duplicant#Morale and +1 Athletics to Duplicants.
Juicer - Each use consumes 1 kg Water, and 250 g of Mushroom, Bristle Berry, and Meal Lice. It grants +4 morale and +1 strength to Duplicants.
Soda Fountain - Each use consumes 5 kg of Water and 1 kg of Carbon Dioxide. It grants +4 morale and +1 Science to Duplicants.
Mechanical Surfboard and Hot Tub utilize water while in use, but do not consume it.
Lavatory, Shower, Wash Basin and Sink use Water and convert it to contaminated Polluted Water.
Carbon Skimmer uses Water to capture Carbon Dioxide and turns it into Polluted Water.
Oil Well requires Water to produce Crude Oil and Natural Gas.
Inside the Apothecary, Duplicants with Medicine Compounding skill can produce Curative Tablet from Coal and Water.
1 kg Coal + 1 kg Water = 1 unit Curative Tablet.

Tips
In most asteroid types, if there is a frozen biome it starts well below the salt water/brine conversion temperature. Piping salt water in is a good way to generate ice from the SW/Brine conversion, as well as cold water/polluted water from the biome's own meltwater. Both the solid and liquid water can then be carried/piped away and used for early game ("Plumbing" is the only required tech) temperature regulation. The brine can be used to create salt or as low-freezing temperature coolant once more advanced technology is researched.
Water can be frozen into a natural tile of Ice. This can be used to create tiles for wild plants, but has limited use due to the low temperatures required.
Although water itself is difficult to produce sustainably, the Petroleum Generator, Natural Gas Generator and Duplicants themselves all produce Polluted Water. This may then be converted into a sustainable source of water.

=Ice=

Production
Cooling Water below its freezing point will turn it into Ice. A water tile less than or equal to 800 kg will turn into ice debris, while a water tile greater than 800 kg will turn into an ice tile.

Cooling Salt Water below its freezing point will turn it into Ice (77% mass) and Brine (23% mass).

Ice Maker can make Ice from Water.

It can be harvested on rocket missions to renewable Space POIs:
In Exploded Ice Giants at a rate of 324 – 972 kg per cycle.
In Frozen Ore Asteroid Fields at a rate of 148 – 443.9 kg per cycle.
In Ice Asteroid Fields at a rate of 135 – 405 kg per cycle.
In Oxygen Rich Asteroid Fields at a rate of 60 – 200 kg per cycle.
In Interstellar Oceans at a rate of 37.5 – 125 kg per cycle.

Usage
A storage of Ice placed in Water pool can help cooling the water.

Ice Block requires Ice to build. It has the highest base decoration value (+20) in the game, together with Marble Block and Metal Block. It will melt in warm environments so its best to build it in the Frozen Biome only.

Ice-E Fan can use Ice to cool the environment. The consumed Ice is melted into bottled Water.

Tips
Mining anything, including ice, will destroy 50% of the original mass. Melting it instead will keep all the mass and double the amount of precious water received but can not be moved as easily.
Ice is generally encountered in biomes with starting temperatures well below the freezing point of pure water.  By piping in heat so as to locally melt ice, the water runoff will often re-freeze as dupe-portable ice.  If the ice is melted with salt water, it is often the case that the temperature exchange will turn the salt water into brine+ice.
Constructing a Tempshift Plate out of Ice will not be affected by the 15°C lower limit of building temperatures. On the other hand, you can only use 20% of the Ice heat capacity that way, as only 20% of buildings mass is considered for heat calculations.
Building a Ice Block in Water will instantly melt the ice block and add the mass of the ice to the water.

=Steam=

Production
Steam naturally comes out of the two types of Geysers, as either 110 °C or 500 °C.
Cool Steam Vents slowly pours lukewarm steam at various rates. At least two uncovered Cool Steam Vents are guaranteed to spawn on each map.
Steam Vent erupts with the large amounts of superheated steam, and is harder to deal with, but can be used directly to power Steam Turbine.

Steam can be created by boiling water, Salt Water, Brine or Polluted Water in hot environment such as Volcanic Biome and Space Biome.
However, Polluted Water produces Dirt when evaporated and Salt Water and brine produce Salt when evaporated.

Usage
Steam naturally cools down to water, one of the important Resources in the game.
Steam of any temperature is used as fuel of Steam Engine for space missions.
Steam of any temperature is used in Sauna for recreational purposes.
Steam Turbine can generate Power from Steam hotter than 125°C. For this reason, the Steam generated by Cool Steam Vent can not be used without additional heating.
Steam can be an alternative for Hydrogen as heat transfer agent in environments above 100 °C since it has better conductivity and heat capacity.

Tips
Steam is an environmental danger and quickly scalds the Duplicants. Better to equip Atmo Suits before entering Steam atmosphere or working with risky water-cooled equipment.
Polluted Water can be cleaned by boiling it into Steam, then condensing it. Directly cooling the Steam to condensation is difficult, as it will damage pipes if done with a Thermo Regulator, and Wheezeworts do not cool below condensation points and will become stifled by hot Steam. Instead, cooling another gas, such as Hydrogen, and using this to cool the Steam, either by bubbling, piping, or using a highly-conductive tile wall between them.
A Liquid Tepidizer can be used to generate Steam if water is dripped onto it (if submerged or in large amounts, the Tepidizer will limit itself before boiling the water). Batteries contained in an insulated room can also reach high temperatures. Alternatively, the bottom of the map contains large amount of very hot material, including Magma. Water pumped onto these hot materials will rapidly boil. However, the resulting Steam will often be extremely hot, making it harder to condense than other methods.
An easy way to generate Steam for Steam Engine is to build a Steam room in Space Biome. The top wall of the room shall be made of Bunker Tile and exposed to sky. The side and bottom wall could be made of normal tiles with good hardness and thermal conductivity. Pumping hot water into this room, and the heat from accumulated Regolith on top ceiling will boil the Water into Steam. A Gas Pump made of Steel can pump the Steam out for Steam Engine.
Another way to generate Steam is to build a normal cooling loop with a Thermal Aquatuner and Radiant Pipes, but no Steam Turbine. Send the loop through a large body of liquid to reheat the coolant and keep the aquatuner running. The heat generated by the Thermal Aquatuner can create steam.

---

## GEYSERS
共 20 篇文档

# 文档：Geyser

- 类别：geysers
- 标识：geyser
- 来源：wiki/Geyser

Geysers are renewable sources of various materials. When active, they alternate between erupting and Idle. The types of geysers, spawned on the map, ultimately decide the economy of the colony.

A Duplicant with the Field Research skill can analyze a geyser in order to figure out its activity duration and dormancy duration.

Dealing with Geysers
Many geysers periodically output a large volume of either heat or troublesome elements when uncovered.

A geyser is considered covered if all of the tiles above the geyser's base are covered. In this state it does not emit anything and cannot be analyzed.

A geyser's type can also be checked by setting their priority to yellow alert with the Priority Tool, then hovering over the yellow alert.

Low temperature geysers can be contained with a simple Insulated Tile box. Volcanoes require at least inner obsidian box (most other materials will eventually melt) and some form of vacuum heat isolation in the long-term.

All geysers' eruptions can be halted by submerging them completely in liquid. Low pressure geysers can be drowned even by gases, and often do it to themselves.

Geyser Variants
All geyser types randomly select an average active yield, eruption periods and percentages, and active periods and percentages; these values are picked independently.

Values in a range are picked based on this formula (graph):
<math display="block">y = \frac{\log_e \left(\frac{1}{0.995054754 x + 0.002472623} - 1.0\right) + 6}{12}</math>

where x is a random value from 0 to 1. A value has approximately 50% chance of being in the middle 20%, and these "likely outcome" ranges are shown on the chart. For example: Most cool slush geysers will output between 1400 kg/cycle (= 2333.33 g/s) and 1600 kg/cycle (= 2666.67 g/s) on average while active.

Possible geyser variants and their parameters are listed in the table below, except for the active amount percentage, which is always between 40% and 80% (the middle 20% of which is between 56% and 64%). The values for parameter ranges are split across rows, with the top (lighter) cell giving the middle 20% of the parameter's range. The bottom (darker) cell lists the full range (100%). Columns with names beginning with an asterisk (＊) indicate a derived value, or a value which is not one of the main randomized parameters of a geyser but which is based on the parameters; the middle 20% threshold for these derived values is based on the middle 20% of their base parameters, not on the middle 20% of the range of the derived value, because these values do not necessarily scale linearly. The calculation of derived values is discussed below.

(sec)

(sec)

(g/sec)

Derived Calculations
A geyser's average active yield (one of their main randomized parameters) is not shown directly to players; nonetheless, it can be derived quite easily using only the geyser's average overall yield (shown in a fully-analyzed geyser's information window under "average output") and its active amount percentage (which is shown under "active period" - e.g. a geyser active for 48.9 cycles every 76.8 cycles has an active amount percentage of roughly 63.7%):

<math>\Delta_{active} = \frac{\Delta_{avg{\%_{active</math>

For example: a Copper Volcano which is active for 48.9 cycles every 76.8 cycles and emits 311.8 g/s on average will have an active yield of 311.8 / 0.637 &approx; 490 g/s; multiplying by 600 gives about 293.7 kg/cycle.

Similarly, it is equally easy to go in reverse: if you have a geyser's average active yield and its active amount percentage, its average overall yield is:

<math>\Delta_{avg} = \Delta_{active} \cdot \%_{active}</math>

Using the same example as above, a Copper Volcano which is active for 48.9 cycles every 76.8 cycles and emits 490 g/s while active on average will have an average overall yield of 490 * 0.637 &approx; 312 g/s; multiplying by 600 gives about 187.2 kg/cycle.

Calculating the eruption rate of a geyser, which is the rate at which the geyser actually emits its contents, is done similarly using the average active yield (see above) and the eruption amount (which is shown under "eruption period" - e.g. a geyser which erupts for 349 seconds every 719 seconds has an active amount percentage of roughly 48.5%):

<math>\Delta_{active} = \Delta_{erupting} \cdot \%_{erupting}</math>
<math>\Delta_{erupting} = \frac{\Delta_{active{\%_{erupting</math>

For example, a Steam Vent which emits 3070.9 g/s of Steam for 349s every 719s will have an active yield of 3070.9 * 0.485 &approx; 1489 g/s (893 kg/cycle) - notably higher than the middle 20% for that parameter. If that same geyser is active for 77.5 cycles every 117.6 cycles (&approx; 66%), then we can calculate its average overall yield to be 1489 * 0.66 &approx; 982 g/s. (The real geyser these values were taken from had an in-game average overall yield of 982.3 g/s.)

Geyser Spawning Rules - Basic Asteroids
All geysers are spawned as part of biomes, with a specified amount for each biome.

Open geysers
Swamp Biome:
One open cool steam vent
One open natural gas vent
Caustic Biome:
One open cool steam vent
One open natural gas OR chlorine vent
Tide Pool Biome:
One open saltwater geyser
Volcanic Biome on Rime Asteroid:
5 open volcanoes
Volcanoes World Trait
8 open volcanoes

Buried geysers
There are 12 randomly spawned buried geysers in each game. The Geoactive World Trait increases the number to 16, and the Geodormant World Trait decreases the number to 9.

These buried geysers are randomly spawned all over the map, except in the start Biome, Volcanic Biome, and Space Biome. These geysers start covered with granite and obsidian. In some cases, maps will contain less than what is listed due to points of interest overwriting each-other due to close proximity, especially in the Oil Biome.

As a convenient rule of thumb, each biome type will only have at most two buried geysers.

Geyser Spawning Rules - Asteroid Clusters (Spaced Out DLC)
Each asteroid within a cluster has a specific list of open geysers, which can be seen by selecting the asteroid in the starmap.

The list of geysers for each asteroid type is as follows:

Sandstone Asteroid

Geyser Probabilities
There are 19 unique geysers to pick from for each of the 12 randomly chosen geysers, each having the same chance of selection. This can be broken down into groups:
Water-producing: 6 (PH2O can be cleaned, steam can be cooled)
Oxygen-producing: 2 (PO2 can be cleaned)
Volcanic: 5 (magma, metal)
Metal-producing: 3
Power-producing: 3 (natural gas, leaky oil, hydrogen)

Ignoring specified geysers (i.e. cool steam vent in swamp), and assuming 9 of the 12 randomly chosen geysers exist on a given world (oil biome geysers tend to not exist), the odds for getting preferred geysers are as follows:

All listed values assume the number of each preferred doesn't matter (two of the same geyser despite preference for more than 1), the odds of getting multiple distinct geysers will be worse.

As an example, if a world with at least two volcanoes is desired, it should have a 73.02% chance per world (5 preferred, 2 wanted). If just want one metal volcano is desired, it should have a 78.70% chance per world (3 preferred, 1 wanted).
